<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчик</a> (21749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимец.html>люби́мец</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubímec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubímčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любимчик.html>люби́мчиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> favorite, pet; teacher's pet; blue-eyed boy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">particularly someone who is manipulative and preys on someone's sympathies to the detriment of others</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>favorite

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зеленый.html>Зелёный</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цвет.html>цвет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zeljónyj — moj <b>ljubímyj</b> cvet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Green is my favorite color.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любитель.html>люби́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любительский.html>люби́тельский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubítelʹskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>amateur, amateurish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">non-professional</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***любить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a> (194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ľubiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewbʰ-</i> whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">love</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полюбить.html>полюби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to love, to like, to be fond of, to grow fond of <i>(more intensely than <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a>)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любоваться.html>любова́ться</a> (4221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любоваться.html>любова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полюбоваться.html>полюбова́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залюбоваться.html>залюбова́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to admire, to feast one's eyes (upon)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubóvʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любовный.html>любо́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljubóvnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)любо́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)любо́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> love
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:любовный.html>любо́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ljubóvnaja</b> istórija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">love story</span></div></dd>

<li>amorous <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">indicating love or sexual desire</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>loving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:любовный.html>любо́вный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгляд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ljubóvnyj</b> vzgljad</i> ― <span class="e-translation">loving glance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любознательность.html>любозна́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljuboznátelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любознательность.html>любозна́тельности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

***любой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любой.html>любо́й</a> (253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ľubъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to like</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ой</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-oj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For semantic shift to "whichever" compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cualquiera</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:любопытно.html>любопы́тно</a> (5248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>curiously, with curiosity</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>one is curious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:любопытно.html>любопы́тно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>ljubopýtno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am curious</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любопытный.html>любопы́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubopýtnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людишки.html>люди́шки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljudíški</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людишки.html>люди́шек</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (worthless) people

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljúdi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***людоед.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:людоед.html>людое́д</a> (9153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljúdi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людоед.html>людое́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljudojéd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людоед.html>людое́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людоед.html>людое́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:людоед.html>людое́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>man-eater, cannibal; a person, animal, or other creature that eats humans</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***люмпен.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:люмпен.html>лю́мпен</a> (23114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lumpen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:люмпен.html>лю́мпен</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljúmpen</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:люмпен.html>лю́мпена</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:люмпен.html>лю́мпены</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:люмпен.html>лю́мпенов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lumpenproletariat" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lumpenproletariat">Lumpenproletariat</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> miscreant, hoodlum, ruffian</li>
<li>snakefish</li></ol>

***лютый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лютый.html>лю́тый</a> (9353)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лютъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljutŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ľutъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***лягнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лягнуть.html>лягну́ть</a> (28005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ляга́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягнуть.html>лягну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljagnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ляга́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to kick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock, to let out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to jump <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to tell something offensive of someone</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шка</a> (6320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ляга́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ljagúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>frog</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> @ (at sign) (more common: <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> "dog")</li></ol>
